The_DT results_NNS show_VBP that_IN the_DT degree_NN of_IN depletion_NN in_IN rinderpest_NN is_VBZ more_JJR than_IN four_CD times_NNS as_RB great_JJ as_IN in_IN acute_JJ theileriasis_NN ._.

SUMMARY_NNP AND_CC CONCLUSIONS_NNP 1_CD ._.
A_DT total_NN of_IN 821_CD wild_JJ T._NNP orientis_NN flies_NNS were_VBD partially_RB fed_VBN on_IN rinderpest_NN infected_VBN animals_NNS and_CC allowed_VBN to_TO complete_VB their_PRP$ feed_NN on_IN a_DT healthy_JJ bull_NN ,_, but_CC the_DT latter_NN did_VBD not_RB develop_VB the_DT infection_NN ._.

H._NNP R._NNP KAPUR_NNP 93_CD Another_DT healthy_JJ bull_NN was_VBD subjected_VBN to_TO only_RB 54_CD infective_JJ bites_NNS and_CC this_DT animal_NN developed_VBD typical_JJ symptoms_NNS of_IN the_DT disease_NN ,_, which_WDT eventually_RB progressed_VBD to_TO a_DT fatal_JJ issue_NN ._.
2_CD ._.
Observations_NNS on_IN the_DT feeding_VBG habits_NNS of_IN T._NNP orientis_NN have_VBP shown_VBN that_IN the_DT fly_NN seldom_RB takes_VBZ more_JJR than_IN one_CD complete_JJ feed_NN in_IN captivity_NN and_CC that_IN ,_, under_IN field_NN conditions_NNS ,_, it_PRP usually_RB enjoys_VBZ an_DT uninterrupted_JJ feed_NN until_IN it_PRP is_VBZ fully_RB engor-_JJ ged_NN ._.
These_DT facts_NNS make_VBP it_PRP impossible_JJ for_IN this_DT fly_NN to_TO play_VB any_DT important_JJ rôle_NN in_IN the_DT spread_NN of_IN rinderpest_NN ._.
3_CD ._.
The_DT virus_NN of_IN rinderpest_NN is_VBZ viable_JJ in_IN the_DT body_NN of_IN the_DT fly_NN for_IN a_DT minimum_JJ period_NN of_IN 30_CD hours_NNS and_CC inert_NN at_IN 48_CD hours_NNS ._.
